add_namespace = annex
add_namespace = annex_ex
country_event = {
	#Check for possible annexations (donotlog)
	id = annex.1
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
	}
	immediate = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				#has_state_flag = annexation_trigger_state
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = occupied_by_@ROOT
				}
			}
			check_potential_annexations = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = AH_checking_for_possible_annexations
	}
}

state_event = {
	#Generic "Land Granted" event
	id = annex.2
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2 FROM = [From.GetName]"
	}
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = annex.2.a
		ROOT = {
			add_political_power = 5
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
			}
		}
	}
}

# Which cores to return?
country_event = {
	id = annex.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3" }
	title = annex.3.t
	desc = annex.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = annex.3.a #return all land
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		clr_country_flag = KR_returning_land
		custom_effect_tooltip = KR_will_return_all
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:return_to = {
				country_event = annex.4
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.3.b #return all land but vital provinces
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				is_important_state = yes
				NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT }
				OR = {
					is_core_of = event_target:return_to
					is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KR_will_return_rest
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = KR_returning_land
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					is_important_state = yes
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:return_to
						is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
						is_important_state = no
						NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT }
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = event_target:return_to }
							is_coastal = yes
						}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = event_target:return_to
							is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:return_to = {
					country_event = annex.4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.3.c #return cores only
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			any_owned_state = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				is_important_state = no
				NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT 	}
				is_core_of = event_target:return_to
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				is_important_state = no
				NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT 	}
				NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:return_to }
				is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KR_will_return_cores
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = KR_returning_land
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT }
					NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:return_to }
					is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
				}
				set_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT
			}
			event_target:return_to = {
				country_event = annex.4
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.3.e #keep it all you pig
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		clr_country_flag = KR_returning_land
		custom_effect_tooltip = KR_will_not_return
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:return_to
						is_claimed_by = event_target:return_to
					}
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT }
				}
				set_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# Cores/claims have been returned by an ally
country_event = {
	id = annex.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.4" }
	title = annex.4.t
	desc = annex.4.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = annex.4.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_returned_land
		}
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = FROM
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					is_claim_or_core_of_FROM = no
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_coastal = yes
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@FROM }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FROM
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					is_claim_or_core_of_FROM = no
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_coastal = yes
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KR_keeping_state@FROM }
				}
				transfer_to_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	country_event = {

	#莱茵兰的命运
	country_event = {
		id = annex.1001
		immediate = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1000 FROM = [From.GetName]"
		}
		title = annexation_RHI_CONQ
		desc = annexation_RHI_CONQ_desc
		is_triggered_only = yes
		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
			}
		}
		option = {
			name = annex.1001.a
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = RHI
				}
				GER = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				GEU = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				WGR = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			GER_state_country_core = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				tag_to_release = RHI
			}
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			#give it to Germany
			name = annex.1001.b
			trigger = {
				var:55.owner = {
					is_germany_tag = yes
					is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				GEU = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				WGR = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				tag_to_release = 55.owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:tag_to_release = {
						original_tag = RHI
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_rhineland = yes
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					}
					transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_rhineland = yes
							is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
						}
						add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
						transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_rhineland = yes
							is_valid_annexation_state = no
						}
						add_claim_by = var:tag_to_release
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_rhineland = yes
						}
						add_core_and_transfer_if_owned_else_add_claim = yes
					}
				}
			}
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			#occupy Rhineland, give the rest to Germany
			name = annex.1001.c
			trigger = {
				is_french_tag = yes
				var:55.owner = {
					is_germany_tag = yes
					is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				GEU = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
				WGR = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 0
			}
			add_state_claim = 42
			add_state_claim = 781
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			set_temp_variable = {
				tag_to_release = 55.owner
			}
			51 = {
				add_core_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes
			}
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			name = annex.1000.d
			trigger = {
				GER = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 6				#Rhineland
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				add_core_of = GER
				transfer_state_to = GER
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			name = annex.1000.e
			trigger = {
				GEU = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 6				#Rhineland
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				add_core_of = GEU
				transfer_state_to = GEU
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			name = annex.1000.f
			trigger = {
				WGR = {
					is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 6				#Rhineland
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				add_core_of = WGR
				transfer_state_to = WGR
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			#occupy
			name = annex.occupation
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_french_tag = no
					and = {
						GEU = {
							is_ally_of_ROOT = no
						}
						GER = {
							is_ally_of_ROOT = no
						}
						WGR = {
							is_ally_of_ROOT = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_french_tag = yes
				}
				add_state_claim = 42
				add_state_claim = 781
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = RHI_CONQ
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
	}

				base = 100

							state = 57
							state = 56
						}

					}
					transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
				}

						limit = {
							or = {
								state = 59
								state = 57
								state = 56
							}
							is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
						}
						add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
						transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
					}

								state = 59
								state = 57
								state = 56
							}
							is_valid_annexation_state = no
						}
						add_claim_by = var:tag_to_release
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {

							or = {
								state = 59
								state = 57
								state = 56
							}
						}
						add_core_and_transfer_if_owned_else_add_claim = yes
					}

				NOT = { country_exists = COG }
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				tag_to_release = COG
			}
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
		option = {
			#occupy
			name = annex.occupation
			trigger = {
				COG = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
			}
			ai_chance = {
				base = 0
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = COG_CONQ
			annexation_event_option_effect = yes
		}
	}
